# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes apimachinery runtime.Object Import Chain

## Your Task

Trace how k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object is imported and used across kubernetes/kubernetes. Find all Go source files in the core/v1 API types that implement runtime.Object by embedding TypeMeta and ObjectMeta, and the files in the API machinery that register these types into the scheme.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Perfect! I've successfully traced the Kubernetes runtime.Object import chain and created a comprehensive analysis. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

**The Import Chain** flows through these main components:

1. **apimachinery--b2e9f88f** (API Machinery library):
   - `pkg/runtime/interfaces.go` - Defines the `Object` interface
   - `pkg/runtime/types.go` - Defines `TypeMeta`
   - `pkg/runtime/register.go` - Implements `ObjectKind` methods on `TypeMeta`
   - `pkg/runtime/scheme.go` - The type registration system
   - `pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go` - Defines `TypeMeta`, `ObjectMeta`, and `ListMeta`

2. **kubernetes--v1.32.0** (Kubernetes core/v1 API):
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` - All core/v1 types that embed TypeMeta and ObjectMeta
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go` - Registers all types into the scheme
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/zz_generated.deepcopy.go` - Auto-generated `DeepCopyObject()` implementations

## How It Works

All core/v1 types implement `runtime.Object` by:
1. **Embedding `metav1.TypeMeta`** - Provides the `GetObjectKind()` method (implemented via `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/register.go`)
2. **Embedding `metav1.ObjectMeta`** (or `ListMeta` for lists) - Provides standard metadata fields
3. **Auto-generated `DeepCopyObject()` methods** - Generated by code generation tools based on `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces` annotations

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete details including 40+ symbol references and a comprehensive narrative explanation.

Chain Analysis\\n\\n## Overview\\nThis trace documents how `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object` interface is defined, implemented, and used across the Kubernetes codebase, specifically tracing Runtime Interface Definition (apimachinery)\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/interfaces.go`\\n- Defines the core `Object` interface:\\n  ```go\\n  type Object interface {\\n    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind\\n    DeepCopyObject() Object\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- This interface is the fundamental contract that all Kubernetes API types must implement to be serializable and manipulatable by the runtime.\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/types.go`\\n- Defines `TypeMeta` struct with:\\n  - `Kind` (string): REST resource type\\n  - `APIVersion` (string): Versioned schema identifier\\n- This is the base type that carries version information for API objects.\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/register.go`\\n- Implements `ObjectKind` interface methods on `TypeMeta`:\\n  - `SetGroupVersionKind()`: Sets Kind and APIVersion on TypeMeta\\n  - `GetObjectKind()`: Returns the ObjectKind (implemented by TypeMeta itself)\\n- This allows any type embedding TypeMeta to satisfy the ObjectKind interface.\\n\\n### 2. Core v1 API Type Definitions (kubernetes)\\n\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`\\n- Defines all core v1 API resource types, which implement runtime.Object by embedding:\\n  - `metav1.TypeMeta`: For GetObjectKind() method\\n  - `metav1.ObjectMeta`: For standard resource metadata\\n\\n**Registered Types** (all implement runtime.Object):\\n- Single Resource Types: Pod, Service, Node, Namespace, ConfigMap, ReplicationController, Event, Endpoints, Secret, ServiceAccount, PersistentVolume, PersistentVolumeClaim, Binding, LimitRange, ResourceQuota, ComponentStatus, PodTemplate\\n- List Types (embed ListMeta): PodList, ServiceList, NodeList, NamespaceList, ConfigMapList, etc.\\n- Options Types: ServiceProxyOptions, PodProxyOptions, PodLogOptions, PodExecOptions, PodAttachOptions, PodPortForwardOptions\\n\\nEach type definition is annotated with `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object` to indicate code generation should create DeepCopyObject() implementations.\\n\\n### 5. Type Registration (kubernetes)\\n\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`\\n- Imports `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime` and defines:\\n  - `SchemeGroupVersion`: Metadata about the v1 group version\\n  - `SchemeBuilder`: Instance of runtime.SchemeBuilder\\n  - `AddToScheme`: Exported function for adding core/v1 types to any scheme\\n- Function `addKnownTypes()` registers all core/v1 types into the scheme via `scheme.AddKnownTypes()`\\n- This registration makes all core/v1 types discoverable by the runtime for serialization/deserialization.\\n\\n### 6. Code Generation (kubernetes)\\n\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/zz_generated.deepcopy.go`\\n- Auto-generated by deepcopy-gen tool\\n- Contains `DeepCopyObject()` implementations for all types marked with `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object`\\n- Implements the second half of the Object interface contract by providing deep-copy functionality\\n\\n## How Core v1 Types Implement runtime.Object\\n\\nAll core/v1 types inherit or provide the two required methods:\\n\\n1. **GetObjectKind()**: Inherited from embedded `metav1.TypeMeta` (implemented in apimachinery/pkg/runtime/register.go)\\n2. **DeepCopyObject()**: Auto-generated in zz_generated.deepcopy.go\\n\\nThis pattern allows the Kubernetes runtime to:\\n- Identify and manage any API object by its Kind/Version\\n- Serialize/deserialize objects to/from JSON or protobuf\\n- Create deep copies for defensive copies or mutations\\n- Work uniformly with all API types regardless of their specific type\\n\\n## Key Files Summary\\n\\n**API Machinery** (Interface and Scheme definitions):\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go`: Object interface definition\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/types.go`: TypeMeta definition\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/register.go`: TypeMeta ObjectKind implementation\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go`: Type registry and management\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go`: TypeMeta, ObjectMeta, ListMeta definitions\\n\\n**Kubernetes Core v1** (Concrete implementations):\\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`: All core v1 resource type definitions\\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`: Type registration into scheme\\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/zz_generated.deepcopy.go`: DeepCopyObject implementations\\n\"\n}\nEOF\ncat /workspace/answer.json\n"

implemented, and used across the Kubernetes codebase, specifically tracing through core/v1 API types and their registration into the runtime scheme.\\n\\n## Detailed Import Chain\\n\\n### 1. Runtime Interface Definition (apimachinery)\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/interfaces.go`\\n- Defines the core `Object` interface:\\n  ```go\\n  type Object interface {\\n    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind\\n    DeepCopyObject() Object\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- This interface is the fundamental contract that all Kubernetes API types must implement to be serializable and manipulatable by the runtime.\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/types.go`\\n- Defines `TypeMeta` struct with:\\n  - `Kind` (string): REST resource type\\n  - `APIVersion` (string): Versioned schema identifier\\n- This is the base type that carries version information for API objects.\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/register.go`\\n- Implements `ObjectKind` interface methods on `TypeMeta`:\\n  - `SetGroupVersionKind()`: Sets Kind and APIVersion on TypeMeta\\n  - `GetObjectKind()`: Returns the ObjectKind (implemented by TypeMeta itself)\\n- This allows any type embedding TypeMeta to satisfy the ObjectKind interface.\\n\\n### 2. Metadata Type Definitions (apimachinery)\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go`\\n- Defines `TypeMeta`: Same as in runtime, used as embedded type in API objects\\n- Defines `ObjectMeta`: Standard metadata for persisted resources\\n  - `Name`: Unique identifier within namespace\\n  - `Namespace`: Namespace the object belongs to\\n  - `UID`: Unique identifier across time and space\\n  - `ResourceVersion`: For optimistic concurrency control\\n  - Plus 30+ other metadata fields (labels, annotations, finalizers, etc.)\\n- Defines `ListMeta`: Metadata for list objects\\n  - `ResourceVersion`: For pagination and watching\\n  - `Continue`: For chunked list results\\n  - `RemainingItemCount`: For list pagination\\n\\n### 3. Scheme and Type Registration (apimachinery)\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/scheme.go`\\n- Defines `Scheme` type that manages:\\n  - `gvkToType`: Maps (Group, Version, Kind) tuples to Go types\\n  - `typeToGVK`: Reverse mapping from Go types to GVK\\n  - Type conversions between different versions\\n  - Serialization/deserialization codecs\\n- The Scheme is the central registry that maintains all known API types and how to work with them.\\n\\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/scheme_builder.go`\\n- Provides `SchemeBuilder`: A builder pattern helper for registering types into a Scheme\\n- Allows multiple registration functions to be composed together\\n\\n### 4. Core v1 API Type Definitions (kubernetes)\\n\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`\\n- Defines all core v1 API resource types, which implement runtime.Object by embedding:\\n  - `metav1.TypeMeta`: For GetObjectKind() method\\n  - `metav1.ObjectMeta`: For standard resource metadata\\n\\n**Registered Types** (all implement runtime.Object):\\n- Single Resource Types: Pod, Service, Node, Namespace, ConfigMap, ReplicationController, Event, Endpoints, Secret, ServiceAccount, PersistentVolume, PersistentVolumeClaim, Binding, LimitRange, ResourceQuota, ComponentStatus, PodTemplate\\n- List Types (embed ListMeta): PodList, ServiceList, NodeList, NamespaceList, ConfigMapList, etc.\\n- Options Types: ServiceProxyOptions, PodProxyOptions, PodLogOptions, PodExecOptions, PodAttachOptions, PodPortForwardOptions\\n\\nEach type definition is annotated with `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object` to indicate code generation should create DeepCopyObject() implementations.\\n\\n### 5. Type Registration (kubernetes)\\n\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`\\n- Imports `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime` and defines:\\n  - `SchemeGroupVersion`: Metadata about the v1 group version\\n  - `SchemeBuilder`: Instance of runtime.SchemeBuilder\\n  - `AddToScheme`: Exported function for adding core/v1 types to any scheme\\n- Function `addKnownTypes()` registers all core/v1 types into the scheme via `scheme.AddKnownTypes()`\\n- This registration makes all core/v1 types discoverable by the runtime for serialization/deserialization.\\n\\n### 6. Code Generation (kubernetes)\\n\\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/zz_generated.deepcopy.go`\\n- Auto-generated by deepcopy-gen tool\\n- Contains `DeepCopyObject()` implementations for all types marked with `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object`\\n- Implements the second half of the Object interface contract by providing deep-copy functionality\\n\\n## How Core v1 Types Implement runtime.Object\\n\\nAll core/v1 types inherit or provide the two required methods:\\n\\n1. **GetObjectKind()**: Inherited from embedded `metav1.TypeMeta` (implemented in apimachinery/pkg/runtime/register.go)\\n2. **DeepCopyObject()**: Auto-generated in zz_generated.deepcopy.go\\n\\nThis pattern allows the Kubernetes runtime to:\\n- Identify and manage any API object by its Kind/Version\\n- Serialize/deserialize objects to/from JSON or protobuf\\n- Create deep copies for defensive copies or mutations\\n- Work uniformly with all API types regardless of their specific type\\n\\n## Key Files Summary\\n\\n**API Machinery** (Interface and Scheme definitions):\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go`: Object interface definition\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/types.go`: TypeMeta definition\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/register.go`: TypeMeta ObjectKind implementation\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go`: Type registry and management\\n- `apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go`: TypeMeta, ObjectMeta, ListMeta definitions\\n\\n**Kubernetes Core v1** (Concrete implementations):\\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`: All core v1 resource type definitions\\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`: Type registration into scheme\\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/zz_generated.deepcopy.go`: DeepCopyObject implementations\\n\"\n}"

Runtime Interface Definition (apimachinery)\n\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/interfaces.go`\n- Defines the core `Object` interface:\n  ```go\n  type Object interface {\n    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind\n    DeepCopyObject() Object\n  }\n  ```\n- This interface is the fundamental contract that all Kubernetes API types must implement to be serializable and manipulatable by the runtime.\n\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/types.go`\n- Defines `TypeMeta` struct with:\n  - `Kind` (string): REST resource type\n  - `APIVersion` (string): Versioned schema identifier\n- This is the base type that carries version information for API objects.\n\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/register.go`\n- Implements `ObjectKind` interface methods on `TypeMeta`:\n  - `SetGroupVersionKind()`: Sets Kind and APIVersion on TypeMeta\n  - `GetObjectKind()`: Returns the ObjectKind (implemented by TypeMeta itself)\n- This allows any type embedding TypeMeta to satisfy the ObjectKind interface.\n\n### 2. Metadata Type Definitions (apimachinery)\n\n**File**: `pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go`\n- Defines `TypeMeta`: Same as in runtime, used as embedded type in API objects\n- Defines `ObjectMeta`: Standard metadata for persisted resources\n  - `Name`: Unique identifier within namespace\n  - `Namespace`: Namespace the object belongs to\n  - `UID`: Unique identifier across time and space\n  - `ResourceVersion`: For optimistic concurrency control\n  - Plus 30+ other metadata fields (labels, annotations, finalizers, etc.)\n- Defines `ListMeta`: Metadata for list objects\n  - `ResourceVersion`: For pagination and watching\n  - `Continue`: For chunked list results\n  - `RemainingItemCount`: For list pagination\n\n### 3. Scheme and Type Registration (apimachinery)\n\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/scheme.go`\n- Defines `Scheme` type that manages:\n  - `gvkToType`: Maps (Group, Version, Kind) tuples to Go types\n  - `typeToGVK`: Reverse mapping from Go types to GVK\n  - Type conversions between different versions\n  - Serialization/deserialization codecs\n- The Scheme is the central registry that maintains all known API types and how to work with them.\n\n**File**: `pkg/runtime/scheme_builder.go`\n- Provides `SchemeBuilder`: A builder pattern helper for registering types into a Scheme\n- Allows multiple registration functions to be composed together\n\n### 4. Core v1 API Type Definitions (kubernetes)\n\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`\n- Defines all core v1 API resource types, which implement runtime.Object by embedding:\n  - `metav1.TypeMeta`: For GetObjectKind() method\n  - `metav1.ObjectMeta`: For standard resource metadata\n\n**Registered Types** (all implement runtime.Object):\n- Single Resource Types: Pod, Service, Node, Namespace, ConfigMap, ReplicationController, Event, Endpoints, Secret, ServiceAccount, PersistentVolume, PersistentVolumeClaim, Binding, LimitRange, ResourceQuota, ComponentStatus, PodTemplate\n- List Types (embed ListMeta): PodList, ServiceList, NodeList, NamespaceList, ConfigMapList, etc.\n- Options Types: ServiceProxyOptions, PodProxyOptions, PodLogOptions, PodExecOptions, PodAttachOptions, PodPortForwardOptions\n\nEach type definition is annotated with `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object` to indicate code generation should create DeepCopyObject() implementations.\n\n### 5. Type Registration (kubernetes)\n\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`\n- Imports `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime` and defines:\n  - `SchemeGroupVersion`: Metadata about the v1 group version\n  - `SchemeBuilder`: Instance of runtime.SchemeBuilder\n  - `AddToScheme`: Exported function for adding core/v1 types to any scheme\n- Function `addKnownTypes()` registers all core/v1 types into the scheme via `scheme.AddKnownTypes()`\n- This registration makes all core/v1 types discoverable by the runtime for serialization/deserialization.\n\n### 6. Code Generation (kubernetes)\n\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/zz_generated.deepcopy.go`\n- Auto-generated by deepcopy-gen tool\n- Contains `DeepCopyObject()` implementations for all types marked with `+k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object`\n- Implements the second half of the Object interface contract by providing deep-copy functionality\n\n## How Core v1 Types Implement runtime.Object\n\nAll core/v1 types inherit or provide the two required methods:\n\n1. **GetObjectKind()**: Inherited from embedded `metav1.TypeMeta` (implemented in apimachinery/pkg/runtime/register.go)\n2. **DeepCopyObject()**: Auto-generated in zz_generated.deepcopy.go\n\nThis pattern allows the Kubernetes runtime to:\n- Identify and manage any API object by its Kind/Version\n- Serialize/deserialize objects to/from JSON or protobuf\n- Create deep copies for defensive copies or mutations\n- Work uniformly with all API types regardless of their specific type\n\n## Key Files Summary\n\n**API Machinery** (Interface and Scheme definitions):\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go`: Object interface definition\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/types.go`: TypeMeta definition\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/register.go`: TypeMeta ObjectKind implementation\n- `apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go`: Type registry and management\n- `apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go`: TypeMeta, ObjectMeta, ListMeta definitions\n\n**Kubernetes Core v1** (Concrete implementations):\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`: All core v1 resource type definitions\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`: Type registration into scheme\n- `kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/zz_generated.deepcopy.go`: DeepCopyObject implementations\n"
